<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:наморщить.html>намо́рщить</a> (15483)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">на-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">na-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:морщить.html>мо́рщить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mórščitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наморщить.html>намо́рщить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">namórščitʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:морщить.html>мо́рщить</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">намо́рщивать</b>)
</p>

***нанесение.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:нанесение.html>нанесе́ние</a> (14955)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">нанес-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nanes-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-е́ние</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-énije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нанесение.html>нанесе́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nanesénije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нанесение.html>нанесе́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нанесение.html>нанесе́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нанесение.html>нанесе́ний</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>putting, inflicting

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:нанести.html>нанести́</a> (3301)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">на-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">na-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нести.html>нести́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nestí</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нанести.html>нанести́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nanestí</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наносить.html>наноси́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to drift (on); to carry, to waft, to deposit, to wash ashore (e.g. of snow, sand, etc.)</li>
<li>to mark (on); to draw (e.g. onto a map)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:нанести.html>нанести́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:карта.html>ка́рту</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nanestí</b> na kártu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to mark/draw on a map</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to inflict (on); to cause (to); to bring
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:нанести.html>нанести́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:оскорбление.html>оскорбле́ние</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nanestí</b> oskorblénije</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to insult</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:нанести.html>нанести́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ущерб.html>уще́рб</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nanestí</b> uščérb</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to cause damage</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:нанести.html>нанести́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:удар.html>уда́р</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nanestí</b> udár</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to strike, to deliver a blow</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to bring <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">too much of something</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>to lay (eggs, a lot)</li>
<li>(<i>in expressions</i>)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:нанести.html>нанести́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:визит.html>визи́т</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nanestí</b> vizít</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to pay a visit</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:нести.html>нёс</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:ти.html>ти́</a></b>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:нанизавший.html>наниза́вший</a> (24147)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">на-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">na-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:носить.html>носи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nosítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наносить.html>наноси́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nanosítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нанести.html>нанести́</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to deposit, to pile up (sand or snow)</li></ol>

<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">нано́с</span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">nanós</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наносить.html>наноси́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nanosítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">нана́шивать</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to bear, to carry <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">in some quantity, in several stages</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:наносить.html>наноси́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:дрова.html>дрова́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nanosítʹ</b> drová</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to carry firewood (a bit at a time)</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
